The decoration of the hotel is good, not sure whether it is four-star or five-star, the hardware is good, there is a swimming pool and gym, although it is not necessary to travel in a hurry, it is better than nothing.
The welcome fruit is directly in the room, no need to rush, there is fruit and two pieces of chocolate, although I didn't eat it and forgot to take it away, but the overall feeling is good.
The mattresses and bedding products are indeed better than those of Express Hotel Atour and All Seasons. My friend's family has a baby, and a crib is also provided. The price for May Day is just over 1100 for a room, which is a little more expensive than Dodo, but this hotel is still more cost-effective. After all, the environment, rooms, supporting facilities, and location are all better.
There are not many varieties of breakfast, and the basics are all there. It‚Äôs just that the attitude of the aunt who cooks eggs is not good. I can give it 4.5 points, and I can stay here next time I come to Taizhou.
